         <h1 class="article_title" itemprop="headline name">
          50 NFL Predictions for the Upcoming 2012 Season
         </h1>
         <h4 class="article_author" itemprop="author">
          <address class="article_author-info" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
           By
           <a class="article_author-link" href="/users/56893-cody-swartz" itemprop="url" title="Cody Swartz">
            <span itemprop="name">
             Cody  Swartz
            </span>
           </a>
           ,
           <span class="author-rank">
            Senior Writer
           </span>
          </address>
          <time class="article_timestamp" data-updated_at="1346646596" itemprop="datePublished">
           Sep 3, 2012
          </time>
         </h4>
         <div id="top-share-buttons-region">

          <header class="article_page-header">

           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:630px">
            <img alt="50 NFL Predictions for the Upcoming 2012 Season" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="http://img.bleacherreport.net/img/slides/photos/002/563/246/hi-res-134293644_crop_north.jpg?w=630&amp;h=420&amp;q=75" width="630"/>

          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            Dont look now, but the official start of the 2012
            <a href="http://bleacherreport.com/nfl">
             NFL
            </a>
            season is less than one week away. By now, you should be memorizing your teams 16-game schedule, finalizing your fantasy drafts and making your season predictions.
           </p>
           <p>
            Preseason has shown us a glimpse of what may be to come this season. The
            <a href="http://bleacherreport.com/articles/1278403-new-york-jets-roster-2012-latest-news-cuts-preseason-predictions">
             New York Jets
            </a>
            will struggle to score points no matter who plays quarterback. The
            <a href="http://bleacherreport.com/articles/1278840-philadelphia-eagles-2012-roster-latest-news-cuts-preseason-predictions">
             Philadelphia Eagles
            </a>
            could be flat-out dominant on their defensive line. Injuries will play a major role in shaping every teams season.
           </p>
           <p>
            What we dont know though is which teams will make the playoffs, who will be the breakout players on each team and who will be the biggest disappointments. This offers just a snapshot of how I think the 2012 season will play out.
           </p>
          </div>
          <a class="paginator paginator--secondary paginator--next" href="javascript: void(0)" title="Begin Slideshow">

          <header class="article_page-header">

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             Cam Newton Will Have a Sophomore Slump
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:630px">
            <img alt="Cam Newton Will Have a Sophomore Slump" data-defer-src="http://img.bleacherreport.net/img/slides/photos/002/563/247/hi-res-150872096_crop_north.jpg?w=630&amp;h=420&amp;q=75" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="630"/>
            <div class="caption-overlay border-box" max-width="630">
            </div>
            <div class="article_image-accreditation" max-width="630">
             <span>
              Jeff Zelevansky/Getty Images
             </span>
             <br/>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            Last year, Cam Newton revolutionized the NFL as a rookie, becoming the first quarterback in history to pass for over 4,000 yards and rush for over 500 in the same season, and he added 35 touchdowns in the processall in a shortened offseason without sufficient time to practice with his new team.
           </p>
           <p>
            I dont think he will be as good in 2012; in fact, I think he will take a significant step back. Newton really benefited from weakened defenses early in the season, and his numbers tailed off down the stretch.
           </p>
           <p>
            He had the fortune of playing 10 games against teams that rated in the bottom half in scoring defense. His numbers against the other six teams: 2-4 record, 56.3 completion percentage and 79.0 passer rating.
           </p>
           <p>
            While people are quick to point out his passing yardage, he was actually 0-3 in games that he threw for over 300 yards and 5-1 in the games with his six lowest passing yardage totals of the season. He rated just 15th in the league in passer rating and 16th in ESPNs new QBR statistic. He was a tremendous runner, but 14 touchdowns just cant happen again; it's unrealistic for a quarterback to run the ball 126 times in a season and not get hurt.
           </p>
           <p>
            Newton is blessed with astounding size, but the
            <a href="http://bleacherreport.com/articles/1287204-carolina-panthers-roster-2012-latest-news-cuts-preseason-predictions">
             Carolina Panthers
            </a>
            know how much he means to them, and theres no way they will let him take off to run that many times again. Steve Smith is another year older, and the team really has no solid No. 2 receiver.
           </p>
           <p>
            I wouldnt be surprised to see Newton add a few passing touchdowns to his totals but throw at least 20 interceptions and post a passer rating slightly worse than last years mark while running for around five or six touchdowns. That would constitute a slump for a player expected to be a top-producing fantasy player at his position already.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>
         <section class="article_page article_page--secondary js-article-page-3 cf display-none " data-page="3">
          <header class="article_page-header">

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             Michael Vick Will Stay Healthy and Have a Career Year
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:630px">
            <img alt="Michael Vick Will Stay Healthy and Have a Career Year" data-defer-src="http://img.bleacherreport.net/img/slides/photos/002/563/248/hi-res-150538957_crop_north.jpg?w=630&amp;h=420&amp;q=75" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="630"/>
            <div class="caption-overlay border-box" max-width="630">
            </div>
            <div class="article_image-accreditation" max-width="630">
             <span>
              Jim Rogash/Getty Images
             </span>
             <br/>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            <a href="http://bleacherreport.com/articles/1315015-is-this-mike-vicks-last-year-as-a-philadelphia-eagle">
            </a>
            <a href="http://bleacherreport.com/michael-vick">
             Michael Vick
            </a>
            s future is on the line in 2012no question about it.The Philadelphia Eagles drafted Nick Foles in the third round of this past years draft, and hes played refreshingly well in the preseason, showing the team
            <a href="http://bleacherreport.com/articles/1217554-philadelphia-eagles-why-nick-foles-is-the-quarterback-of-the-future">
             he has the tools to be the quarterback of the future
            </a>
            .
           </p>
           <p>
            Vick has played all 16 games in a season just once in his career, and hes already suffered two near-injuries in preseason. Hes also 32 years old, and hes a running quarterback with a notorious history of getting hurtbut I think 2012 will be his best year yet.
           </p>
           <p>
            I see Vick staying healthy for 15 of 16 games this season, passing for over 3,500 yards and throwing 25 touchdowns. Hes also a terrific runner and will probably add five or six rushing touchdowns to his totals, and that makes him one of the most dangerous weapons in the NFL.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>
         <section class="article_page article_page--secondary js-article-page-4 cf display-none " data-page="4">
          <header class="article_page-header">
           <div class="article_nav-bar br-texture--sudo br-texture--sudo-fade-to-white">
            <div class="paginators paginators--top">

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             Maurice Jones-Drew Will Struggle
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:630px">
            <img alt="Maurice Jones-Drew Will Struggle" data-defer-src="http://img.bleacherreport.net/img/slides/photos/002/563/249/hi-res-136320090_crop_north.jpg?w=630&amp;h=420&amp;q=75" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="630"/>
            <div class="caption-overlay border-box" max-width="630">
            </div>
            <div class="article_image-accreditation" max-width="630">
             <span>
              Al Messerschmidt/Getty Images
             </span>
             <br/>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            This really isnt that bold of a prediction at all, but I would be saying this even if there hadn't been a holdout.
           </p>
           <p>
            Maurice Jones-Drew rushed for over 1,600 yards in 2011 on an offense with a struggling rookie quarterback and a limited supporting cast of receivers. He averaged over 100 yards on the ground per game while playing against mostly eight- and nine-man boxes.
           </p>
           <p>
            Now hes entering his seventh season and has nearly 1,500 career carries on his resumeand hes coming off a season in which he led the NFL with 343 carries and 386 touches. Hell be lucky to get 1,000 rushing yards after this holdout.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>
         <section class="article_page article_page--secondary js-article-page-5 cf display-none " data-page="5">
          <header class="article_page-header">
           <div class="article_nav-bar br-texture--sudo br-texture--sudo-fade-to-white">

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             Brandon Lloyd Will Top 1,500 Receiving Yards
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:630px">
            <img alt="Brandon Lloyd Will Top 1,500 Receiving Yards" data-defer-src="http://img.bleacherreport.net/img/slides/photos/002/563/250/hi-res-150079932_crop_north.jpg?w=630&amp;h=420&amp;q=75" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="630"/>
            <div class="caption-overlay border-box" max-width="630">
            </div>
            <div class="article_image-accreditation" max-width="630">
             <span>
              Jim Rogash/Getty Images
             </span>
             <br/>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            I really like the
            <a href="http://bleacherreport.com/articles/1280417-new-england-patriots-roster-2012-latest-news-cuts-preseason-predictions">
             New England Patriots
            </a>
             acquisition of Brandon Lloyd. He had a breakout season with the
            <a href="http://bleacherreport.com/articles/1281528-denver-broncos-roster-2012-latest-news-cuts-preseason-predictions">
             Denver Broncos
            </a>
            in 2010, leading the NFL with 1,448 receiving yards, and now that he has
            <a href="http://bleacherreport.com/tom-brady">
             Tom Brady
            </a>
            and plays in an offense with
            <a href="http://bleacherreport.com/wes-welker">
             Wes Welker
            </a>
            , Rob Gronkowski and Aaron Hernandez, he should have an even better year in 12.
           </p>
           <p>
            Lloyd will likely be a Pro Bowler, and he should put up 1,500 yards or more with a dozen touchdowns in an offense that scores at least 500 points.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>
         <section class="article_page article_page--secondary js-article-page-6 cf display-none " data-page="6">
          <header class="article_page-header">
           <div class="article_nav-bar br-texture--sudo br-texture--sudo-fade-to-white">

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             Jake Locker Will Be an MVP Candidate
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:630px">
            <img alt="Jake Locker Will Be an MVP Candidate" data-defer-src="http://img.bleacherreport.net/img/slides/photos/002/563/251/hi-res-151020410_crop_north.jpg?w=630&amp;h=420&amp;q=75" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="630"/>
            <div class="caption-overlay border-box" max-width="630">
            </div>
            <div class="article_image-accreditation" max-width="630">
             <span>
              Joe Murphy/Getty Images
             </span>
             <br/>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            He hasnt gotten a lot of hype heading into 2012, but I think the
            <a href="http://bleacherreport.com/articles/1280605-tennessee-titans-roster-2012-latest-news-cuts-preseason-predictions">
             Tennessee Titans
            </a>
            made the right choice going with Jake Locker as their quarterback.
           </p>
           <p>
            Locker was a first-round pick in 11, and he inherits a team with a pretty solid offenseKenny Britt, Nate Washington, Kendall Wright, Jared Cook and Chris Johnsonplus a very fine offensive line that includes two bookend offensive tackles and newly signed guard Steve Hutchinson.
           </p>
           <p>
            Locker played sparingly as a rookie last year but he accounted for five total touchdowns (four passing, one rushing) without turning the ball over once. I think he will lead the Titans to the playoffs this year, putting up around 25 touchdown passes through the air and five or so rushing touchdowns.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>

              <span class="paginators_page-count">

              </span>
             </a>
            </div>
            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             Marcell Dareus Will Be Unblockable
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:630px">
            <img alt="Marcell Dareus Will Be Unblockable" data-defer-src="http://img.bleacherreport.net/img/slides/photos/002/563/252/hi-res-131140575_crop_north.jpg?w=630&amp;h=420&amp;q=75" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="630"/>
            <div class="caption-overlay border-box" max-width="630">
            </div>
            <div class="article_image-accreditation" max-width="630">
             <span>
              Rick Stewart/Getty Images
             </span>
             <br/>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            Marcell Dareus is not a sexy pick, but hes my candidate to win the 2012 NFL Defensive Player of the Year award.
           </p>
           <p>
            Dareus quietly had a spectacular season for the
            <a href="http://bleacherreport.com/articles/1284631-buffalo-bills-roster-2012-latest-news-cuts-preseason-predictions">
             Buffalo Bills
            </a>
            after they made him the third overall pick in last years draft, and now that he plays on a defensive line that features Mario Williams and Mark Anderson in addition to Kyle Williams, Dareusand the Billswill be extremely tough on defense.
           </p>
           <p>
            Dareus can play defensive end, defensive tackle or nose tackle. Last year, he registered 5.5 sacks and 24 quarterback pressures as a pass-rusher while picking up 32 solo tackles and 31 stops as a run-stopper.
           </p>
           <p>
            Dareus is a mammoth force at 63, 319 pounds, and hes going to be difficult for one man to contain. I think he will finish with around a dozen sacks, a pile of forced fumbles and an overall presence that helps the Bills make the playoffs.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>
         <section class="article_page article_page--secondary js-article-page-8 cf display-none " data-page="8">
          <header class="article_page-header">
           <div class="article_nav-bar br-texture--sudo br-texture--sudo-fade-to-white">
            <div class="paginators paginators--top">

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             Billieve in the Bills
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:630px">
            <img alt="Billieve in the Bills" data-defer-src="http://img.bleacherreport.net/img/slides/photos/002/563/253/hi-res-150436731_crop_north.jpg?w=630&amp;h=420&amp;q=75" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="630"/>
            <div class="caption-overlay border-box" max-width="630">
            </div>
            <div class="article_image-accreditation" max-width="630">
             <span>
              Hannah Foslien/Getty Images
             </span>
             <br/>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            I really like the blueprint for the 2012 Buffalo Billstheyre preparing to win games in the trenches, and they have the talent to do so. The interior offensive line is one of the best in the game with Andy Levitre and Eric Wood as Pro Bowl-caliber players, and the defensive line rivals that of the
            <a href="http://bleacherreport.com/articles/1281948-2012-new-york-giants-roster-latest-news-cuts-and-preseason-predictions">
             New York Giants
            </a>
            and Philadelphia Eagles for the NFLs best.
           </p>
           <p>
            The Bills signed Pro Bowl defensive end Mario Williams to a six-year deal (although they overpaid him) and grabbed Mark Anderson (10 sacks in 2011) from the New England Patriots to go with Kyle Williams and Marcell Dareus, two players that are already unblockable themselves.
           </p>
           <p>
            The Bills should put up 50 or more sacks this year, and Im going out on a limb and saying Dareus is my NFL Defensive Player of the Year pick.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>
         <section class="article_page article_page--secondary js-article-page-9 cf display-none " data-page="9">

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             Tim Tebow Wont Be the Answer in New York
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:630px">
            <img alt="Tim Tebow Wont Be the Answer in New York" data-defer-src="http://img.bleacherreport.net/img/slides/photos/002/563/254/hi-res-151014464_crop_north.jpg?w=630&amp;h=420&amp;q=75" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="630"/>
            <div class="caption-overlay border-box" max-width="630">
            </div>
            <div class="article_image-accreditation" max-width="630">
             <span>
              Jeff Zelevansky/Getty Images
             </span>
             <br/>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            Im extremely interested to see what happens with
            <a href="http://bleacherreport.com/mark-sanchez">
             Mark Sanchez
            </a>
            and
            <a href="http://bleacherreport.com/tim-tebow">
             Tim Tebow
            </a>
            in New York (and is there any chance Greg McElroy plays into the picture?).
           </p>
           <p>
            I think Sanchez will start all 16 games, believe it or not, but I wouldnt be surprised to see Tebow playing entire quarters at some point. However, I dont think Tebow will be the answer in New York for several reasons.
           </p>
           <p>
            First of all, hes not very good. His completion percentage suggests he should be playing a different position, and hes liable to get injured with how much he runs.
           </p>
           <p>
            Second, I dont think the team is as good as the Jets think. They lack explosive pass-rushers, the right tackle position could cost them and the wide receivers and running backs are subpar.
           </p>
           <p>
            Tebow might run for six or seven touchdowns and make some nice third- and fourth-down conversions, but hes not going to get the Jets to the playoffs, and hes not the long-term answer.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>
         <section class="article_page article_page--secondary js-article-page-10 cf display-none " data-page="10">
          <header class="article_page-header">

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             The 2011 NFL Draft Will Go Down as One of the Best Ever
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:630px">
            <img alt="The 2011 NFL Draft Will Go Down as One of the Best Ever" data-defer-src="http://img.bleacherreport.net/img/slides/photos/002/563/255/hi-res-113276819_crop_north.jpg?w=630&amp;h=420&amp;q=75" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="630"/>
            <div class="caption-overlay border-box" max-width="630">
            </div>
            <div class="article_image-accreditation" max-width="630">
             <span>
              Justin Edmonds/Getty Images
             </span>
             <br/>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            I cant believe how good the first-round picks from last years draft played just as rookies. Cam Newton and Von Millerthe first two pickswon the Offensive Rookie and Defensive Rookie of the Year awards.
           </p>
           <p>
            In fact, nearly every team has to be feeling really good about its top-10 pick. Marcell Dareus, A.J. Green, Patrick Peterson, Julio Jones, Aldon Smith and Tyron Smith all look like the kind of players that teams can build their franchises around.
           </p>
           <p>
            I think Jake Locker will have a great year, and players like Robert Quinn and J.J. Watt could each be on the verge of putting themselves on the list of top 10 players at their position.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             5 Quarterbacks Will Get Benched This Season
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:630px">
            <img alt="5 Quarterbacks Will Get Benched This Season" data-defer-src="http://img.bleacherreport.net/img/slides/photos/002/563/256/hi-res-150739357_crop_north.jpg?w=630&amp;h=420&amp;q=75" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="630"/>
            <div class="caption-overlay border-box" max-width="630">
            </div>
            <div class="article_image-accreditation" max-width="630">
             <span>
              Thearon W. Henderson/Getty Images
             </span>
             <br/>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            Carson Palmer, Blaine Gabbert, John Skelton, Brandon Weeden and Ryan Tannehill will all get benched at some point this season.
           </p>
           <p>
            The
            <a href="http://bleacherreport.com/articles/1280504-oakland-raiders-roster-2012-latest-news-cuts-preseason-predictions">
             Oakland Raiders
            </a>
            drastically overpaid for Palmer, and theyre about to realize its time to move on from him and maybe give
            <a href="http://bleacherreport.com/terrelle-pryor">
             Terrelle Pryor
            </a>
            a shot. Gabbert, Weeden and Tannehill will fall under the classification of quarterbacks pushed into the starting spot too soon, and Skelton just isnt very good at all.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             A.J. Green Will Lead the NFL in Receiving Yards
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:630px">
            <img alt="A.J. Green Will Lead the NFL in Receiving Yards" data-defer-src="http://img.bleacherreport.net/img/slides/photos/002/563/257/hi-res-131648094_crop_north.jpg?w=630&amp;h=420&amp;q=75" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="630"/>
            <div class="caption-overlay border-box" max-width="630">
            </div>
            <div class="article_image-accreditation" max-width="630">
             <span>
              Andy Lyons/Getty Images
             </span>
             <br/>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            The
            <a href="http://bleacherreport.com/articles/1281724-cincinnati-bengals-roster-2012-latest-news-cuts-preseason-predictions">
             Cincinnati Bengals
            </a>
            picked A.J. Green with the fourth overall pick in the 2011 NFL draft, and they got a Pro Bowl season from him already as a rookie.
           </p>
           <p>
            Green caught 65 passes for 1,057 yards and seven touchdowns from rookie quarterback Andy Dalton in his first season, and I think hes poised to become arguably the best receiver in the league by the conclusion of 2012.
           </p>
           <p>
            Green is hands down the No. 1 target on his team, and I envision him catching around 100 balls for more than 1,500 yards and 12 touchdowns.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             Tom Brady Will Win Another MVP
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:630px">
            <img alt="Tom Brady Will Win Another MVP" data-defer-src="http://img.bleacherreport.net/img/slides/photos/002/563/258/hi-res-150712915_crop_north.jpg?w=630&amp;h=420&amp;q=75" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="630"/>
            <div class="caption-overlay border-box" max-width="630">
            </div>
            <div class="article_image-accreditation" max-width="630">
             <span>
              Al Messerschmidt/Getty Images
             </span>
             <br/>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            The New England Patriots enter 2012 with an offense that could challenge the undefeated 2007 club for offensive dominance.
           </p>
           <p>
            They return Rob Gronkowski, Aaron Hernandez and Wes Welker, while adding playmaking receiver Brandon Lloyd, who led the National Football League in receiving yards (1,448) in 2010. The offensive line is stout, and the team gets the luxury of
            <a href="http://espn.go.com/blog/nflnation/post/_/id/56896/2012-nfl-strength-of-schedule">
             playing the easiest schedule in the league in 2012
            </a>
            .
           </p>
           <p>
            Tom Brady may be 35 years old, but he has shown zero signs of declining. Hes coming off a season in which he threw for 5,235 passing yards, 39 touchdowns and just 12 interceptions, while posting a 105.6 passer rating. Brady plays in a system fit to maximize his potential, and youre going to see it this season.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             Tyron Smith Will Start for the NFC in the Pro Bowl (For the Next Decade)
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:630px">
            <img alt="Tyron Smith Will Start for the NFC in the Pro Bowl (For the Next Decade)" data-defer-src="http://img.bleacherreport.net/img/slides/photos/002/563/259/hi-res-134134754_crop_north.jpg?w=630&amp;h=420&amp;q=75" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="630"/>
            <div class="caption-overlay border-box" max-width="630">
            </div>
            <div class="article_image-accreditation" max-width="630">
             <span>
              Ronald Martinez/Getty Images
             </span>
             <br/>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            The
            <a href="http://bleacherreport.com/articles/1282093-dallas-cowboys-roster-2012-latest-news-cuts-preseason-prediction">
             Dallas Cowboys
            </a>
            made a terrific move when they selected offensive tackle Tyron Smith with their first-round selection in the 2011 NFL draft, and theyre going to be reaping the rewards for the next decade or more.
           </p>
           <p>
            Smith was one of the top tackles in the league already as a rookie last year, finishing as the fifth-best player at his position in the National Football League (
            <a href="https://www.profootballfocus.com/data/by_position.php?tab=by_position&amp;season=2011&amp;pos=T&amp;stype=r&amp;runpass=&amp;teamid=-1&amp;numsnaps=25&amp;numgames=1">
             per Pro Football Focus
            </a>
            ).He showed signs of dominance as both a run-blocker and pass-blocker, and hes only going to get better in year two.
           </p>
           <p>
            The NFC doesnt have the elite offensive tackles that it did in the days of Orlando Pace and Walter Jones, and with Jason Peters Achilles injury, Smith is almost a lock to make the Pro Bowl this season. Once he makes it and gets his name out there, hes going to make it every yearor as long as the Pro Bowl exists.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             There Will Be No Reason to Ever Watch a Jacksonville Jaguars Game
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:630px">
            <img alt="There Will Be No Reason to Ever Watch a Jacksonville Jaguars Game" data-defer-src="http://img.bleacherreport.net/img/slides/photos/002/563/260/hi-res-150695177_crop_north.jpg?w=630&amp;h=420&amp;q=75" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="630"/>
            <div class="caption-overlay border-box" max-width="630">
            </div>
            <div class="article_image-accreditation" max-width="630">
             <span>
              Patrick Smith/Getty Images
             </span>
             <br/>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            The
            <a href="http://bleacherreport.com/articles/1286232-jacksonville-jaguars-roster-2012-latest-news-cuts-preseason-predictions">
             Jacksonville Jaguars
            </a>
            have an absolutely pitiful offense, and the team might not have scored a point all season without Maurice Jones-Drew ending his holdout.
           </p>
           <p>
            Realistically, they will probably stumble to 200 points or so by default, but theyre going to be bad. Blaine Gabbert showed nothing positive as a rookie, and Im not a fan of their selection of wide receiver Justin Blackmon in the first round. The other receiving targets are mediocre players like Laurent Robinson, Brian Robiskie, Cecil Shorts and tight end Marcedes Lewis.
           </p>
           <p>
            Pencil them in for anywhere from two to four wins and a top-five pick in the 2013 NFL draft.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>
         <section class="article_page article_page--secondary js-article-page-16 cf display-none " data-page="16">

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             The Philadelphia Eagles Will Register 60 Sacks
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:630px">
            <img alt="The Philadelphia Eagles Will Register 60 Sacks" data-defer-src="http://img.bleacherreport.net/img/slides/photos/002/563/261/hi-res-136319857_crop_north.jpg?w=630&amp;h=420&amp;q=75" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="630"/>
            <div class="caption-overlay border-box" max-width="630">
            </div>
            <div class="article_image-accreditation" max-width="630">
             <span>
              Patrick McDermott/Getty Images
             </span>
             <br/>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            Last year, the Philadelphia Eagles and
            <a href="http://bleacherreport.com/articles/1280836-minnesota-vikings-roster-2012-latest-news-cuts-preseason-predictions">
             Minnesota Vikings
            </a>
            tied for the NFL lead with 50 sacks. The year before, the
            <a href="http://bleacherreport.com/articles/1281920-pittsburgh-steelers-roster-2012-latest-news-cuts-preseason-predictions">
             Pittsburgh Steelers
            </a>
            led the league with 48 sacks. The last teams to register 60 sacks were the 2006
            <a href="http://bleacherreport.com/articles/1281785-san-diego-chargers-roster-2012-latest-news-cuts-preseason-predictions">
             San Diego Chargers
            </a>
            (61) and the 2006
            <a href="http://bleacherreport.com/articles/1282263-baltimore-ravens-roster-2012-latest-news-cuts-preseason-predictions">
             Baltimore Ravens
            </a>
            (60).
           </p>
           <p>
            The Eagles have a defensive line that is the best in the league and could be for them what the New York Giants had last year. Trent Cole and Jason Babin are nearly unstoppable pass-rushers, and the backups behind themBrandon Graham, Vinny Curry and Phillip Huntcould probably start for most teams.
           </p>
           <p>
            On the interior line, Mike Patterson may not play this season, but Cullen Jenkins and Derek Landri are a fine starting duo, Fletcher Cox is a Pro Bowler in the making and Antonio Dixon and Cedric Thornton give the team strong depth.
           </p>
           <p>
            The Eagles have 19 sacks in the preseason already, and thats without Babinand Cole hasnt played much either.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>
         <section class="article_page article_page--secondary js-article-page-17 cf display-none " data-page="17">
          <header class="article_page-header">
           <div class="article_nav-bar br-texture--sudo br-texture--sudo-fade-to-white">

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             The San Francisco 49ers Will Stumble to 9-7
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:630px">
            <img alt="The San Francisco 49ers Will Stumble to 9-7" data-defer-src="http://img.bleacherreport.net/img/slides/photos/002/563/262/hi-res-150808695_crop_north.jpg?w=630&amp;h=420&amp;q=75" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="630"/>
            <div class="caption-overlay border-box" max-width="630">
            </div>
            <div class="article_image-accreditation" max-width="630">
             <span>
              Justin Edmonds/Getty Images
             </span>
             <br/>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            The
            <a href="http://bleacherreport.com/articles/1278366-san-francisco-49ers-roster-2012-latest-news-cuts-preseason-predictions">
             San Francisco 49ers
            </a>
            wont be as good in 2012 simply because Jim Harbaugh squeezed every drop of talent he could out of the team in 2011.
           </p>
           <p>
            Alex Smith had a career year, the defense stayed remarkably healthyall 11 starters started at least 13 games, and nine started 15 or more and the team went 7-2 in close games, a rate that very likely wont carry over to 2012, considering the NFL average is 50 percent and its been proven that winning close games does not correlate from year to year.
           </p>
           <p>
            The division is betterthe
            <a href="http://bleacherreport.com/articles/1281029-seattle-seahawks-roster-2012-latest-news-cuts-preseason-predictions">
             Seattle Seahawks
            </a>
            have an underrated defense, as do the
            <a href="http://bleacherreport.com/articles/1283273-arizona-cardinals-2012-latest-news-roster-cuts-preseason-predictions">
             Arizona Cardinals
            </a>
            . The 49ers will probably be in the hunt for the NFC West title all year, but I dont see them emerging as champions.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>
         <section class="article_page article_page--secondary js-article-page-18 cf display-none " data-page="18">
          <header class="article_page-header">
           <div class="article_nav-bar br-texture--sudo br-texture--sudo-fade-to-white">
            <div class="paginators paginators--top">

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             Sam Bradford Will Show Signs That He Is the Next David Carr
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:630px">
            <img alt="Sam Bradford Will Show Signs That He Is the Next David Carr" data-defer-src="http://img.bleacherreport.net/img/slides/photos/002/563/263/hi-res-150832777_crop_north.jpg?w=630&amp;h=420&amp;q=75" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="630"/>
            <div class="caption-overlay border-box" max-width="630">
            </div>
            <div class="article_image-accreditation" max-width="630">
             <span>
              Ronald Martinez/Getty Images
             </span>
             <br/>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            After a solid enough rookie season in 2010,
            <a href="http://bleacherreport.com/sam-bradford">
             Sam Bradford
            </a>
            showed major signs of regression in 2011, throwing for just six touchdowns and a 70.5 passer rating while winning one of 10 games.
           </p>
           <p>
            His offensive line is truly atrociousRodger Saffold is a disastrous left tackle, and former second overall pick Jason Smith was bad enough at right tackle that the team just traded him to the New York Jets for an equally as bad right tackle (Wayne Hunter). Last year, the Rams gave up a league-high 55 sacks after allowing just 34 in 2010.
           </p>
           <p>
            If the Rams line is as bad in 2012, Bradford will look like the next David Carra talented quarterback who will be done in by his inept offensive line.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>
         <section class="article_page article_page--secondary js-article-page-19 cf display-none " data-page="19">
          <header class="article_page-header">
           <div class="article_nav-bar br-texture--sudo br-texture--sudo-fade-to-white">

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             Peyton Manning Wont Be as Good as People Think
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:630px">
            <img alt="Peyton Manning Wont Be as Good as People Think" data-defer-src="http://img.bleacherreport.net/img/slides/photos/002/563/264/hi-res-150812425_crop_north.jpg?w=630&amp;h=420&amp;q=75" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="630"/>
            <div class="caption-overlay border-box" max-width="630">
            </div>
            <div class="article_image-accreditation" max-width="630">
             <span>
              Justin Edmonds/Getty Images
             </span>
             <br/>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            <a href="http://bleacherreport.com/peyton-manning">
             Peyton Manning
            </a>
            is a 36-year-old quarterback coming off four major neck surgeries in the last two seasons. Hes going to a team that had the ninth-worst scoring defense in the league and an offensive line that rated ninth-worst in the league in pass-blocking and dead last in run-blocking,
            <a href="https://www.profootballfocus.com/data/by_team.php?tab=by_team">
             according to Pro Football Focus
            </a>
            .
           </p>
           <p>
            The running game is headed by a 31-year-old back who had a career year under a running quarterback in 2011, and Manning will have to learn a new offense in a new system. He
            <a href="http://profootballtalk.nbcsports.com/2012/08/14/peyton-manning-im-36-my-arm-isnt-the-same-as-when-i-was-22/">
             doesnt have the arm strength he had back in his prime
            </a>
            , and he
            <a href="http://espn.go.com/blog/nflnation/post/_/id/56896/2012-nfl-strength-of-schedule">
             inherits a schedule that ranks second-toughest in the NFL
            </a>
            . Oh, and he goes from playing his home games in a dome to outdoors.
           </p>
           <p>
            I actually worry about Mannings long-term health after this season. Hes taken quite a beating during his career. I think Manning will probably throw for about 3,500 yards and 20-25 touchdowns simply because thats almost the norm for quarterbacks these days. But hes nowhere near a league MVP candidate anymore.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>
         <section class="article_page article_page--secondary js-article-page-20 cf display-none " data-page="20">
          <header class="article_page-header">

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             Chad Johnson Will Be Irrelevant
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:630px">
            <img alt="Chad Johnson Will Be Irrelevant" data-defer-src="http://img.bleacherreport.net/img/slides/photos/002/563/265/hi-res-150130990_crop_north.jpg?w=630&amp;h=420&amp;q=75" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="630"/>
            <div class="caption-overlay border-box" max-width="630">
            </div>
            <div class="article_image-accreditation" max-width="630">
             <span>
              J. Meric/Getty Images
             </span>
             <br/>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            I started compiling the topics for this article several weeks ago, and Chad Johnson being irrelevant has already happened, as the
            <a href="http://bleacherreport.com/articles/1278175-miami-dolphins-roster-2012-latest-news-cuts-preseason-predictions">
             Miami Dolphins
            </a>
            released the former six-time Pro Bowler.
           </p>
           <p>
            Johnson technically could still sign with an NFL franchise, but I would seriously question the motives behind a team signing him. He didnt make any impact at all for the New England Patriots in 2011, and at the age of 34 with his best days clearly behind him, he may have to find an Arena Football team if he wants to keep playing.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>
         <section class="article_page article_page--secondary js-article-page-21 cf display-none " data-page="21">
          <header class="article_page-header">

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             Jared Cook Will Be the AFCs Next Great Tight End
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:630px">
            <img alt="Jared Cook Will Be the AFCs Next Great Tight End" data-defer-src="http://img.bleacherreport.net/img/slides/photos/002/563/266/hi-res-150257720_crop_north.jpg?w=630&amp;h=420&amp;q=75" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="630"/>
            <div class="caption-overlay border-box" max-width="630">
            </div>
            <div class="article_image-accreditation" max-width="630">
             <span>
              Otto Greule Jr/Getty Images
             </span>
             <br/>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            Jared Cook is a popular fantasy sleeper pick heading into 2012 for the way he broke out down the stretch last year, and Im fully on board that bandwagon.
           </p>
           <p>
            In his final three games, Cook averaged seven receptions for 112 yards and caught a touchdown. He finished with 49 receptions for 759 yards and three touchdowns in 2011, and I think he could put up 1,000 yards this year.
           </p>
           <p>
            Kenny Britt cant stay healthyor out of troubleand Kendall Wright is a rookie, which means quarterback Jake Locker may feel most comfortable with Cook as an intermediate target.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>
         <section class="article_page article_page--secondary js-article-page-22 cf display-none " data-page="22">
          <header class="article_page-header">
           <div class="article_nav-bar br-texture--sudo br-texture--sudo-fade-to-white">
            <div class="paginators paginators--top">

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             The Seattle Seahawks Will Lead the NFC in Scoring Defense
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:630px">
            <img alt="The Seattle Seahawks Will Lead the NFC in Scoring Defense" data-defer-src="http://img.bleacherreport.net/img/slides/photos/002/563/267/hi-res-135785364_crop_north.jpg?w=630&amp;h=420&amp;q=75" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="630"/>
            <div class="caption-overlay border-box" max-width="630">
            </div>
            <div class="article_image-accreditation" max-width="630">
             <span>
              Jay Drowns/Getty Images
             </span>
             <br/>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            The Seattle Seahawks dont have a big-name defense, but they have the ability to be really good in 2012. Their defensive line is extremely solid with players like Red Bryant, Alan Branch, Chris Clemons and Brandon Mebane, plus Bruce Irvin rushing the passer from the outside linebacker position.
           </p>
           <p>
            The secondary is probably the NFLs best: Brandon Browner picked off six passes last year and made the Pro Bowl, Richard Sherman held opposing quarterbacks to a 46.4 completion percentage and 57.3 passer rating and Kam Chancellor and Earl Thomas are the best safety duo in the league.
           </p>
           <p>
            The team finished seventh in the league in scoring defense in 2011 and ninth in total defense. Considering the Seahawks get to face Kevin Kolb/John Skelton, Sam Bradford and Alex Smith six times this yearplus Ryan Fitzpatrick, Mark Sanchez and Ryan Tannehill for another threethey have no excuses not to finish as a top-five defense this year.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             Problems on the Offensive Line Will Cost Norv Turner His Job
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:630px">
            <img alt="Problems on the Offensive Line Will Cost Norv Turner His Job" data-defer-src="http://img.bleacherreport.net/img/slides/photos/002/563/268/hi-res-151020983_crop_north.jpg?w=630&amp;h=420&amp;q=75" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="630"/>
            <div class="caption-overlay border-box" max-width="630">
            </div>
            <div class="article_image-accreditation" max-width="630">
             <span>
              Thearon W. Henderson/Getty Images
             </span>
             <br/>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            <a href="http://bleacherreport.com/norv-turner">
             Norv Turner
            </a>
            probably should have been fired in 2010 and definitely in 2011, so the fact that hes still around for the 2012 season is absolutely perplexing.
           </p>
           <p>
            The San Diego Chargersdespite an immensely talented offensive unit with
            <a href="http://bleacherreport.com/philip-rivers">
             Philip Rivers
            </a>
            and Antonio Gateshavent so much as made a Super Bowl during Turners tenure, and theyve missed the playoffs for two years running.
           </p>
           <p>
            The team is in trouble on the offensive line heading into this year, as longtime offensive linemen Marcus McNeill and Kris Dielman each retired during the offseason, and
            <a href="http://www.nctimes.com/sports/football/professional/nfl/chargers/chargers-gaither-has-mri-on-ailing-back-as-concern-over/article_b690e375-0994-5b59-b455-28d2d9bee595.html">
             new left tackle Jared Gaither cant stay healthy
            </a>
            .
           </p>
           <p>
            Thats bad news for the Chargers, especially considering right guard Louis Vasquez and right tackle Jeromey Clary are awful players. Rivers may spend more time on his back than standing upright this season, and that will cost Turner his job.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>
         <section class="article_page article_page--secondary js-article-page-24 cf display-none " data-page="24">
          <header class="article_page-header">
           <div class="article_nav-bar br-texture--sudo br-texture--sudo-fade-to-white">

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             Morris Claiborne Will Be a Godsend for the Dallas Cowboys
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:630px">
            <img alt="Morris Claiborne Will Be a Godsend for the Dallas Cowboys" data-defer-src="http://img.bleacherreport.net/img/slides/photos/002/563/269/hi-res-143684013_crop_north.jpg?w=630&amp;h=420&amp;q=75" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="630"/>
            <div class="caption-overlay border-box" max-width="630">
            </div>
            <div class="article_image-accreditation" max-width="630">
             <span>
              Al Bello/Getty Images
             </span>
             <br/>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            What a draft-day trade the Dallas Cowboys pulled off when they traded up to select future All-Pro corner Morris Claiborne, the one man who will give DeSean Jackson, Hakeem Nicks and Victor Cruz trouble in the future.
           </p>
           <p>
            The Cowboys were beaten constantly with Terence Newman and Orlando Scandrick in 2011, but now they have Claiborne and free-agent acquisition Brandon Carr from the
            <a href="http://bleacherreport.com/articles/1281504-kansas-city-2012-latest-news-cuts-preseason-predictions">
             Kansas City Chiefs
            </a>
            . Claiborne has the physical tools to excel immediately in this league, and I think he will make his fair share of Pro Bowls between now and 2025.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>
         <section class="article_page article_page--secondary js-article-page-25 cf display-none " data-page="25">
          <header class="article_page-header">
           <div class="article_nav-bar br-texture--sudo br-texture--sudo-fade-to-white">
            <div class="paginators paginators--top">

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             Asante Samuel Will Lead the NFL in Interceptions
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:630px">
            <img alt="Asante Samuel Will Lead the NFL in Interceptions" data-defer-src="http://img.bleacherreport.net/img/slides/photos/002/563/270/hi-res-151066077_crop_north.jpg?w=630&amp;h=420&amp;q=75" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="630"/>
            <div class="caption-overlay border-box" max-width="630">
            </div>
            <div class="article_image-accreditation" max-width="630">
             <span>
              Kevin C. Cox/Getty Images
             </span>
             <br/>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            The
            <a href="http://bleacherreport.com/articles/1280028-atlanta-falcons-roster-2012-latest-news-cuts-preseason-predictions">
             Atlanta Falcons
            </a>
            picked up a tremendously talented ball-hawk corner in Asante Samuel for just a seventh-round pick, and its going to pay off for them in 2012.
           </p>
           <p>
            The NFL is a passing league, and having three good cornerbacks is almost a must. Samuel gives the Falcons a terrific trio, and hes got a natural feel for the ball that will carry over. Samuel has picked off at least six passes in four of the past six seasons, and he has led the league on two occasions.
           </p>
           <p>
            This will be his third such time leading the NFL. Ill say eight picks, two returned for touchdowns, and another pick-six in the playoffs.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>
         <section class="article_page article_page--secondary js-article-page-26 cf display-none " data-page="26">
          <header class="article_page-header">
           <div class="article_nav-bar br-texture--sudo br-texture--sudo-fade-to-white">
            <div class="paginators paginators--top">
             <a class="paginator paginator--secondary paginator--prev" href="javascript: void(0)" title="Previous Page">

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             Eli Manning Will Have His Best Year Yet
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:630px">
            <img alt="Eli Manning Will Have His Best Year Yet" data-defer-src="http://img.bleacherreport.net/img/slides/photos/002/563/271/hi-res-151044108_crop_north.jpg?w=630&amp;h=420&amp;q=75" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="630"/>
            <div class="caption-overlay border-box" max-width="630">
            </div>
            <div class="article_image-accreditation" max-width="630">
             <span>
              Rich Schultz/Getty Images
             </span>
             <br/>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            I still dont think
            <a href="http://bleacherreport.com/eli-manning">
             Eli Manning
            </a>
            is an elite quarterback yet. This is a quarterback who threw a league-high 25 interceptions as recently as 2010, and he still put up some dud games last yearjust check out his performances against the last-place
            <a href="http://bleacherreport.com/articles/1280122-washington-redskins-roster-2012-latest-news-cuts-preseason-predictions">
             Washington Redskins
            </a>
            both times.
           </p>
           <p>
            I think he will be at his all-time best in 2012 though. Manning threw for 4,933 yards, 29 touchdowns and 16 interceptions and set NFL records for fourth-quarter comebacks (seven) and game-winning drives (eight) in a season.
           </p>
           <p>
            Now that he has Rueben Randle in addition to Hakeem Nicks and Victor Cruz, Manning has weapons that would make almost every quarterback in the league jealous.
           </p>
           <p>
            Passing yards dont correlate to victories nearly as much as people think, but I think Manning will still put up 4,500 yards or so on at least 8.5 yards per attempt with 30-35 touchdown passes and no more than 15 interceptions. His passer rating last year was just 92.9, which wasnt even his career best, but I think he will approach 100 in 2012.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>
         <section class="article_page article_page--secondary js-article-page-27 cf display-none " data-page="27">
          <header class="article_page-header">

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             Jay Cutler to Brandon Marshall Will Be Like the Old Days
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:630px">
            <img alt="Jay Cutler to Brandon Marshall Will Be Like the Old Days" data-defer-src="http://img.bleacherreport.net/img/slides/photos/002/563/272/hi-res-150462972_crop_north.jpg?w=630&amp;h=420&amp;q=75" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="630"/>
            <div class="caption-overlay border-box" max-width="630">
            </div>
            <div class="article_image-accreditation" max-width="630">
             <span>
              Jonathan Daniel/Getty Images
             </span>
             <br/>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            The
            <a href="http://bleacherreport.com/articles/1283948-chicago-bears-roster-2012-latest-news-cuts-preseason-predictions">
             Chicago Bears
            </a>
            made an incredible move when they sent a pair of third-rounders to Miami for playmaking wide receiver
            <a href="http://bleacherreport.com/brandon-marshall">
             Brandon Marshall
            </a>
            , which reunites Marshall with his old Denver quarterback,
            <a href="http://bleacherreport.com/jay-cutler">
             Jay Cutler
            </a>
            .
           </p>
           <p>
            Cutler to Marshall was one of the leagues best QB-WR duos back in the day, and I think they will recapture their magic in 2012. Marshall will be helped by Devin Hester and Alshon Jeffery, and I see him picking up close to 100 catches for 1,300 yards and 10 touchdowns.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>
         <section class="article_page article_page--secondary js-article-page-28 cf display-none " data-page="28">
          <header class="article_page-header">
           <div class="article_nav-bar br-texture--sudo br-texture--sudo-fade-to-white">
            <div class="paginators paginators--top">

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             The Cincinnati Bengals Will Repeat Their 2011 Success
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:630px">
            <img alt="The Cincinnati Bengals Will Repeat Their 2011 Success" data-defer-src="http://img.bleacherreport.net/img/slides/photos/002/563/273/hi-res-105996282_crop_north.jpg?w=630&amp;h=420&amp;q=75" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="630"/>
            <div class="caption-overlay border-box" max-width="630">
            </div>
            <div class="article_image-accreditation" max-width="630">
             <span>
              Kevin C. Cox/Getty Images
             </span>
             <br/>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            The Cincinnati Bengals surprised the world by winning nine games in 2011 with a rookie QB and rookie WR, and I think they will win the division in 2012.
           </p>
           <p>
            I think Andy Dalton will take a step back; he really underachieved down the stretch, especially as he faced elite defenses like the Pittsburgh Steelers and Baltimore Ravens twice each. But A.J. Green is an absolute stud, and Jermaine Gresham is a Pro Bowl tight end.
           </p>
           <p>
            The offensive line is very stoutespecially the offensive tacklesand the defense did rank very well in many key areas in 2011, finishing ninth in scoring defense, seventh in total defense and fourth in adjusted net passing yards per attempt.
           </p>
           <p>
            The Steelers are aging, and their offensive line will be subpar with Mike Adams underachieving so far in preseason and David DeCastro likely out for the season, plus Mike Wallace has had a lengthy holdout. The Ravens are missing Terrell Suggs, their offensive line took a hit when Ben Grubbs left in free agency and they cant rely on
            <a href="http://bleacherreport.com/ray-lewis">
             Ray Lewis
            </a>
            and Ed Reed forever.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>
         <section class="article_page article_page--secondary js-article-page-29 cf display-none " data-page="29">
          <header class="article_page-header">
           <div class="article_nav-bar br-texture--sudo br-texture--sudo-fade-to-white">

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             Ray Rice Will Set the NFL Single-Season Record for Yards from Scrimmage
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:630px">
            <img alt="Ray Rice Will Set the NFL Single-Season Record for Yards from Scrimmage" data-defer-src="http://img.bleacherreport.net/img/slides/photos/002/563/274/hi-res-150694909_crop_north.jpg?w=630&amp;h=420&amp;q=75" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="630"/>
            <div class="caption-overlay border-box" max-width="630">
            </div>
            <div class="article_image-accreditation" max-width="630">
             <span>
              Patrick Smith/Getty Images
             </span>
             <br/>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            I love the way Ray Rice fits into the Baltimore Ravens offense, and I think he will have a big year to show for it in 2012.
           </p>
           <p>
            Rice rushed for 1,364 yards and 12 touchdowns last year, while adding 76 receptions for 704 yards out of the backfield, giving him a total of 2,068 yards from scrimmage, which led the NFL.
           </p>
           <p>
            I think he will be even more of a focal point of the Ravens offense this year, rushing for close to 1,600 yards and adding just over 900 out of the backfield on receptions, just edging Chris Johnsons 2009 mark of 2,509 yards from scrimmage in a single season.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>
         <section class="article_page article_page--secondary js-article-page-30 cf display-none " data-page="30">
          <header class="article_page-header">
           <div class="article_nav-bar br-texture--sudo br-texture--sudo-fade-to-white">

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             Blaine Gabbert Wont Show Any Improvement
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:630px">
            <img alt="Blaine Gabbert Wont Show Any Improvement" data-defer-src="http://img.bleacherreport.net/img/slides/photos/002/563/275/hi-res-150695168_crop_north.jpg?w=630&amp;h=420&amp;q=75" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="630"/>
            <div class="caption-overlay border-box" max-width="630">
            </div>
            <div class="article_image-accreditation" max-width="630">
             <span>
              Patrick Smith/Getty Images
             </span>
             <br/>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            The Jacksonville Jaguars reached for Blaine Gabbert in the first round of the 2011 NFL draft and then all but threw him under the bus when they made him the starting quarterback in Week 3 with a receiving corps that included players like a washed-up Mike Sims-Walker, Jason Hill, Cecil Shorts and Chastin West.
           </p>
           <p>
            What in the world were they thinking? Gabbert didnt help their case by shying away from contact and looking like a player who had never played the position before, but I blame the Jacksonville Jaguars for pushing him into the starting role when he wasnt ready.
           </p>
           <p>
            I dont see Justin Blackmon playing well as a rookie, which means Gabbert will struggle again; itll probably be Chad Henne time by Week 7 in Jacksonville.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>
         <section class="article_page article_page--secondary js-article-page-31 cf display-none " data-page="31">
          <header class="article_page-header">
           <div class="article_nav-bar br-texture--sudo br-texture--sudo-fade-to-white">
            <div class="paginators paginators--top">

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             Randy Moss Will Make a Positive Impact on the San Francisco 49ers
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:630px">
            <img alt="Randy Moss Will Make a Positive Impact on the San Francisco 49ers" data-defer-src="http://img.bleacherreport.net/img/slides/photos/002/563/276/hi-res-151072274_crop_north.jpg?w=630&amp;h=420&amp;q=75" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="630"/>
            <div class="caption-overlay border-box" max-width="630">
            </div>
            <div class="article_image-accreditation" max-width="630">
             <span>
              Justin Edmonds/Getty Images
             </span>
             <br/>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            After spending most of 2010 bouncing from team to team and 2011 out of the NFL,
            <a href="http://bleacherreport.com/randy-moss">
             Randy Moss
            </a>
            signed on with the San Francisco 49ers this year.
           </p>
           <p>
            The team has a logjam at wide receivertheres
            <a href="http://bleacherreport.com/michael-crabtree">
             Michael Crabtree
            </a>
            , first-round pick A.J. Jenkins, Ted Ginn Jr., Mario Manningham and Moss. Tight end Vernon Davis is actually a better target than any of those players, and I think he will be Alex Smiths go-to guy again.
           </p>
           <p>
            However, I think Moss could put up 30 to 40 catches for maybe 450 yards and four touchdowns. That wont be anything close to the player that made the Pro Bowl so many times during his prime, but its much better than what counterpart wide receivers
            <a href="http://bleacherreport.com/terrell-owens">
             Terrell Owens
            </a>
            and Chad Johnson are doing at this point in their careers.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>
         <section class="article_page article_page--secondary js-article-page-32 cf display-none " data-page="32">
          <header class="article_page-header">
           <div class="article_nav-bar br-texture--sudo br-texture--sudo-fade-to-white">
